-- create the database studentdatabase
CREATE SCHEMA `studentdatabase` ;

-- create the tables

-- card_in table
CREATE TABLE `card_id` (
  `tag` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `studentNumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `surname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `student_number` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- clockedin table
CREATE TABLE `clockedin` (
  `user` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tag` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `attendee` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `timestamp` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `weekday` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `time` time(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `hour` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `date` date NOT NULL,
  `faculty` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `department` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `subject_code` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `attendee_count` bigint DEFAULT NULL,
  `student_attendance_rate` double NOT NULL,
  `student_number` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- scanit table
CREATE TABLE `scanit` (
  `tag` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `student_number` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `surname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `age_group` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `department` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- subjects table 
CREATE TABLE `subjects` (
  `subject_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `subject_code` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `subject_credit` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `department` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `faculty` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `semester_type` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `departement` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- user table
CREATE TABLE `user` (
  `name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `surname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `id` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `number` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `position` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `user_device` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `picture` longblob,
  UNIQUE KEY `ID` (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- visitors table
CREATE TABLE `visitors` (
  `name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `building` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `TimeIn` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `TimeOut` text NOT NULL,
  `visited` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_in` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_out` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- Fill the tables

-- card_in table
